# Names.txt adds name- and industry-related pools according to Vic2 culture
# It is not necessary, but it can help with immersion
# If a culture lacks an entry, the converter will output a line to remind you

# [Vic2 culture] = {
#     first_names = { [pool of male names] }
#     last_names = { [pool of surnames] }
#     female_names = { [pool of female names] }
#     female_surnames = { [pool of female surnames] }
#     callsigns = { [pool of callsigns] }
#     industry_companies = { [pool of industry companies names] }
#     electronic_companies = { [pool of electronic companies names] }
#     car_companies = { [pool of car companies names] }
#     naval_companies = { [pool of naval companies names] }
#     weapon_companies = { [pool of weapon companies names] }
#     aircraft_companies = { [pool of aircraft companies names] }
#     intelligence_agencies = { [pool of spy agencies names] }

# Female surnames is used in those cultures where a surname can change according
# to gender, e.g. Russian, where Vladimir Putin's wife is Lyudmila Putina (née Shkrebneva)
# If a specific female surnames pool is not defined here, the male one will be used

# As the space is used to separate entries in the pool, enclose an entry with space in it using
# quotation marks. E.g. von Berlin is understood as two different entries, 'von' and 'Berlin';
# "von Berlin", instead, is understood as one entry 'von Berlin'

# Do not be shy with diacritical marks, just be sure that HoI4 displays them

# For ease of use, this file is sorted alphabetically according to culture strings

# Supports Vanilla Vic2, HPM and the EU4Vic2 converter project

### NOTE TO SELF: in case of empty input name pools, the generated country leader
### is named "Nomen Nescio" (from Latin, "I don't know the name")
